NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
I, A. Raj Kiran, Biological son of Thiru A. Upendra Gupta residing at No. 45 Nattu Pilliyar Koil Street, Sowcarpet,
Chennai-600 001. Through the way of this public notice, I inform that (late) G. Venkatesam Chetty and G.V. Vasundaramma
has legally adopted me as their son by the way of registered deed bearing the No. 237, dated 20th September 1996
at Sub Register Office, Sowcarpet, Chennai-600 001.
My Adopted Father Thiru G. Venkatesam Chetty (late), has passed away on 14th February 2007.
Here after I shall be known as G.V. Raj Kiran instead of A. Raj Kiran.
Chennai, 18th May 2015.

A. RAJ KIRAN.

U. Udhayalingam was born as a male child to M. Udhayakumar, on 17th May 1992, residing at No. 14, 2nd Street,
Burma Colony, Ekkattuthangal, Chennai-600 032. After an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery, she has been living as
a female (Reference Dr. Jayaraman Department of Plastic Reconstructive, Faciomaxillary and Cosmetic Surgery, Government
General Hospital, Chennai-600 003). The plant surgery show that I could be treated as a Female. U. Udhayalingam shall
henceforth be known as U. MAANCY.
Chennai, 21st May 2015.

U. UDHAYALINGAM.

PRINTED AND PUBLISHED BY THE DIRECTOR OF STATIONERY AND PRINTING, CHENNAI
ON BEHALF OF THE GOVERNMENT OF TAMIL NADU
